What is really different Is the fact that you can post any kind of transaction or accounting adjustment in a single entry, and get it registered in journal, accounts receivable, accounts payable, sales book, purchases book.\r\nMaybe it doesn´t seem important but you can delete any account of the chart of accounts at any moment, having it been posted or not. \r\nAll set up is made in the chart of account, it can be performed account by account.
